Current Affairs Commentary

The Significance of Germany Abolishing Free Navigation Clauses 66

— Yu

The Treaty of Versailles has finally become a "dead letter." In recent years, every move in German diplomacy has been enough to affect France, the midwife of "Versailles," the League of Nations, the offspring of "Versailles," Czechoslovakia, another byproduct of Versailles, and the Soviet Union, which has a deep relationship with all three. Recently, the German government notified the governments of fourteen countries, announcing the abolition of the clauses stipulated in Part XII of the Treaty of Versailles regarding the international free navigation of rivers within Germany, such as the Rhine, Oder, Elbe, Niemen, Danube, and Kiel Canal. We can also observe the impact of this move from the above-mentioned aspects. Of course, Germany had long ago made up its mind to completely tear up the Treaty of Versailles. In 1932, the year before the Nazi Party came to power, we saw at the Lausanne Conference the Germans abolish the reparations that the current Minister of Economy, Hjalmar Schacht, considered "draining the blood of the German people." In 1933, Germany demanded equal status and withdrew from the League of Nations. In 1935, Germany abolished the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles in order to expand its military. In 1936, Germany abolished the Locarno Security Pact while arming the Rhineland. The current abolition of international free navigation on rivers within Germany is a consistent tactic of the Nazi Party, and in terms of foreign policy, it is a response to other fascist countries and an expression of opposition to the European peace front. Since the establishment of the German-Austrian Agreement in July, the two European fascist countries have not been as critical of each other as they were in the past two years due to the struggle for hegemony over Austria. Recently, Foreign Minister Ciano visited Berlin. As a result, not only did the two countries bury the hatchet, but they also established many secret agreements in political and economic terms. That is, with regard to Austria, they reached an understanding; with regard to the Danube River economic issues, they divided spheres of influence; with regard to the future Locarno Conference, they adopted unified action, contacted Britain to put pressure on France, weakened the forces of the peace front, and created an anti-Soviet war fund. Since Germany and Italy already have close ties, Germany naturally wants to respond in unison to Italy's diplomatic actions. The result of the tripartite meeting between Italy, Austria, and Hungary on the 12th of this month was that the protocol recognized that Austria and Hungary have the right to demand equal rights to armaments. This is no less than another serious blow to the Treaty of Versailles. Germany, having a tacit understanding in advance, must also have an expression later. The abolition of the clauses on international free navigation has become a timely embellishment.

After Germany abolishes the clauses on international free navigation, the countries most affected will of course be Switzerland and Czechoslovakia, because both of these countries are landlocked and must pass through international rivers to reach the sea. According to Part XII of the Treaty of Versailles, several international committees were established to manage the Rhine, Oder, Elbe, Niemen, and Danube Rivers. The purpose was to provide convenience to these countries. Now that Germany has unilaterally abolished the international navigation clauses, Czechoslovakia will have no way to utilize the international waterways of the Elbe and Danube Rivers, and will also have no way to access the free ports of Hamburg and Stettin within Germany. In this sense, Czechoslovakia has indeed suffered a not small blow. From another perspective, giving Czechoslovakia a direct blow is also giving France an indirect demonstration, because among the Little Entente countries, Czechoslovakia is France's most loyal ally and the closest friend of the Soviet Union. Germany wants to expand its power in Central Europe, promote its eastward development policy, and unite the European Germanic nations into a great Germanic empire. All of them need to strike at the "thorn in the eye" of Central Europe. Moreover, in today's rising anti-peace movement in Central Europe, cunning Nazis also need an excuse to lift the shackles of the Treaty of Versailles from the Germanic nation in order to divert the attention of the hungry masses at home.

Spanish Rebel Army Launches a Full-Scale Attack on Madrid; Aerial Bombardment and Cannon Fire Resound Ceaselessly; the Besieged City's Garrison Repulsed in Three Counterattacks 67

(London) The Spanish Nationalist army is currently bombarding the gates of Madrid. According to the latest news from the Nationalist army, they have found a weakness in the defensive lines laid by the government forces, which they had been seeking for days. As for the bridges that were blown up in the area where the Nationalist army crossed the river, it did not actually hinder their advance, because the Manzanares River is extremely shallow, only about two feet deep, and the troops can simply wade across the river. The Nationalist army's advance from the north not only allows them to attack the western defensive lines of the government forces from the rear, but also provides a flat road for tanks and other vehicles to drive straight into Madrid.

It is reported that the headquarters of Nationalist army commander General Varela has moved to the Cuatro Vientos airfield, only about four miles from the center of Madrid. Before the Nationalist army attacked, they first opened fire with heavy artillery, and at the same time, several of their bombers dropped more than fifty tons of bombs on the government forces, causing fires in many places with flames soaring. A Reuters reporter in the Nationalist army reported in a telegram that the fighting was extremely fierce and the sound of machine guns never stopped for even half an hour. The government forces' artillery positions in Madrid opened fire with heavy artillery, and the Nationalist army returned fire in kind. Moorish soldiers and legionnaires charged with bayonets and captured a ridge held by the government forces.

According to a Reuters correspondent in the Nationalist army, eight Nationalist bombers, led by twenty-four fighters, dropped one ton of bombs near the University City of Madrid and Casa de Campo, causing a violent bombardment. The government forces were forced to abandon their original defense positions. After the heavy bombardment, the area was filled with smoke that lingered for a long time. Three government planes participated in the battle and were very brave, flying very low over the Nationalist army's positions and strafing the enemy with machine guns. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

Avila. Spanish rebel forces launched a full-scale attack on Madrid's western gate this morning, intending to enter the capital city from the Montaña barracks and the Modelo prison. The rebel artillery also bombarded that area fiercely on the eve of the attack, with ceaseless cannon fire all night long. Rebel planes dropped multiple bombs on the old Royal Palace, and the university district and French Bridge outside the city were also targeted for bombing. (National Telegraph, 16th)

Madrid. The Defense Committee declared at noon today that rebel forces near Madrid had not crossed the Manzanares River at any point. Moroccan soldiers and legionnaires belonging to the rebel forces, under the cover of nineteen tanks, engaged our forces near the "French" bridge (two kilometers north of Casa de Campo Park) west of the city starting at 3:00 PM yesterday, but after four hours of fierce fighting, they ultimately failed to reach their objective and retreated with heavy losses. Our forces demolished the "French" bridge and destroyed three tanks. The intensity of the fighting was unprecedented since the beginning of the battles near Madrid. This morning, the rebel forces attacked again, but were again repulsed by our forces. In addition, rebel planes flew to the capital yesterday and dropped bombs, killing many civilians. It is said that the rebel forces' native Spanish pilots are unwilling to drop bombs over the capital, so the bombers are German and Italian pilots. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Avila. Our correspondent reports exclusively that the government forces yesterday made another attempt to break through the Nationalist army's lines on the outskirts of Madrid, but failed again. The government forces adopted a feint attack strategy, initially pretending to attack the area of the "Toledo" bridge outside the southern gate, with intense gunfire and artillery fire, but soon unexpectedly launched a surprise attack on the San Isidro Cemetery area in the southwestern suburbs. This area was defended by two columns of legionnaires under the command of Nationalist army Colonels De la Torre and Baron. When the legionnaires saw the enemy forces attacking, they hid behind the hillside and tried their best to resist, and fired machine guns from the side. As a result, the government forces could not withstand it and immediately retreated to their original positions. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Seville. The Nationalist army's radio station in this city recently issued a battle report stating that the government forces' three counterattacks near Madrid yesterday all failed, leaving more than 400 bodies behind. A Frenchman named Blanc was also killed in action. The first counterattack by the government forces was carried out by the so-called "International Brigade," whose members were mostly from Russia and Catalonia, carrying the latest Russian weapons, and attacked the Nationalist army's right flank (south of Madrid), but were defeated and heavily damaged by the Nationalist army. The second counterattack, also in the town of Alcala, was repulsed. The Nationalist army took the opportunity to use tanks to attack the Toledo bridge area, inflicting heavy casualties on the government forces. Finally, the government forces launched counterattacks at the Toledo, Princesa, Segovia bridgeheads, but were forced to retreat after heavy artillery fire from the Nationalist army. The Nationalist army immediately occupied the town of Pozuelo on the outskirts of the city and carried out mopping-up operations in the area already occupied south of Madrid. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Spanish Prime Minister Expresses Determination to Resist, Says Loss of Madrid Unrelated to Overall War Situation 68

Valencia. Prime Minister Caballero, having just returned from an inspection of the front lines in Madrid, gave a statement to our reporter saying that the soldiers and civilians of Madrid are determined to fight to the end, and the capital will certainly not fall into the hands of the rebel army. Fascism is deeply hated by the Spanish people, and there is no possibility of success. Even if Madrid falls, the rebel army will only gain a moral victory, which is unrelated to the overall war situation. In short, we are determined to defend every inch of land in our hands with all our strength, until we die in battle. As for the weapons we need, they are now arriving in a steady stream, so it would not be wrong to say that the war has only just begun. In addition, the people of the whole country are against the rebel army, and the final victory will undoubtedly belong to us. Our reporter then asked if the Spanish government planned to recapture the Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean, which had been occupied by the Nationalist army and where the Italians had built strong defensive fortifications. The Prime Minister replied, "The Spanish government will never give up its legitimate territory. The war will continue until all the territory before the civil strife has been restored." (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Rebel Air Raids Over Madrid Three Times a Day; Nearly One Hundred Dead, Three Hundred Wounded 69

Madrid. After bombing Madrid this morning, Nationalist army planes flew over again around 3:00 PM for a second attack, dropping bombs. The sky was clear and boundless. From the ground, it was clear that there were two squadrons of Nationalist bombers, protected by fighters, flying quite high. The bombs they dropped were the same as this morning, mostly falling in the densely populated "Quadrilateral District." It was Sunday afternoon, and many residents were walking and sunbathing along the Pablo Iglesias Avenue in that area. They were suddenly attacked by enemy planes dropping bombs and could not escape to the basement in time. As a result, ten people were killed and about one hundred were wounded. They were immediately carried into ambulances and private cars and transported to be buried or to various hospitals for treatment. The doctors in the hospitals were insufficient, so private doctors were temporarily invited to help. In total, in the last 24 hours, 80 to 100 people have died due to Nationalist army air raids, and 300 have been wounded, many of whom may die from their injuries or have become disabled. It is also reported that during this morning's Nationalist army air raid, a bomb destroyed the roof of the Faculty of Law. In addition, the Nationalist army used heavy artillery to bombard various districts of Madrid, relentlessly throughout the day. In the afternoon, the Plaza de España and the most modern Gran Vía in the city center were also hit by multiple shells. Although the residents of the city are living in a hail of bullets, their morale is still very high and they are not discouraged at all. After the enemy's repeated air raids, the soldiers and civilians defending the city are even more hostile to the enemy, and their morale is even higher. The government has posted notices all over the streets, calling on the soldiers and civilians to bravely resist and saying that the government forces will soon be able to win and save the people from their suffering. Although the crowds on the streets are under the threat of enemy planes and artillery shells, they seem not to be afraid at all, and there are still many people reading the notices aloud in various places. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Madrid. According to a communiqué issued here today, the Nationalist army launched three air raids on the capital today, killing 17 people and wounding more than 100. The first air raid involved ten bombers and twelve fighters, dropping many bombs. One bomb landed in the Central University, and the rest landed in the North Station and densely populated areas, causing many casualties. Government planes took off to attack, but the enemy planes retreated without a fight. According to reports in today's newspapers, there is fully confirmed news that in the past two weeks, government planes have shot down 100 Nationalist army planes. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Fierce Battle in Southern Suburbs of the Capital; Rebel Left Wing Crosses River; West Park Occupied 70

Talavera. According to a Reuters correspondent in the Nationalist army, the two sides are still engaged in fierce fighting along a ten-mile front. The former Royal Private Garden, Casa de Campo, is still the main battlefield for seizing the capital. Last night, 200 militiamen used ropes to climb the walls of the garden and attacked the Nationalist army's sentry posts. It is reported that three Englishmen were among the dead. All 200 were wiped out, but the defending forces also suffered heavy losses. Well-trained soldiers in the militia then attacked the column commanded by Colonel Castelljon, which was holding part of Casa de Campo, but failed due to the lack of artillery support. Further north, the Nationalist army column commanded by Colonel Barón has occupied several houses near the Segovia Bridge. It is believed that the government army machine gunners defending the area have retreated to the Madrid side of the Manzanares River. Fierce fighting continued in various locations south of Madrid throughout yesterday. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

Salamanca. The Nationalist army headquarters recently issued a communiqué stating that three columns under the command of General Varela of the Central Army yesterday afternoon crossed the Manzanares River outside Madrid and immediately occupied many of the defensive fortifications built by the government forces. Earlier, our army bravely attacked at dawn yesterday, and the enemy stubbornly resisted, and the war was very fierce. However, the enemy artillery was controlled by our artillery fire, and our infantry, under the cover of tanks and aircraft, rushed through the Casa de Campo Park west of the city. The enemy was facing the river to fight, resisting desperately. Our army was in high morale, and fought the enemy in close combat with bayonets and hand grenades, and finally occupied several of the enemy's defensive fortifications, and captured several tanks. The enemy then collapsed and retreated, and our army was able to advance to the northwestern area of Madrid. By evening, it had occupied the West Park and the Calle de los Rosales (north of the North Station), which was the most important battle yesterday. No major battles occurred on other fronts. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Government Aircraft Active Everywhere, Bombarding Enemy Positions Vigorously 71

Madrid. The Ministry of Aviation recently announced that government aircraft were active everywhere yesterday from morning to night, carrying out bombardments. The details are as follows:

(1) Multiple government aircraft first flew to the Avila airfield (90 kilometers from the capital) west of the capital and saw seven rebel bombers and three fighters parked there, all made in Germany. They immediately bombarded them and then flew to the Dorioux and Toledo airfields in the south to carry out bombardments. (2) The Talavera railway station, 100 kilometers southwest of the capital, is a key strategic location. Government aircraft also bombarded it. (3) The area near the Casa de Campo Park in the western suburbs is where a large number of rebel forces are concentrated. (3) The necessary expenses will be included in the supplementary budget for the current year. (4) The purpose of this agency is to fully acquire the functions of the Economic Planning Board. (16th Kyodo News)

(Tokyo) The outline of the national policy integration agency decided by the Four Ministers Conference is as follows: (1) To establish a large-scale national policy planning agency within the Cabinet, including the Investigation Bureau, Resources Bureau, Statistics Bureau, and Information Committee affiliated with the current Cabinet. (2) The name is yet to be determined, possibly the Cabinet General Affairs Agency. (3) The head of this agency will be a specially appointed official or treated as such. When necessary, they may attend Cabinet meetings as a Minister of State. (4) This agency will have the functions of the Economic Planning Board, responsible for establishing comprehensive plans for economic and industrial control. (5) The organization of this agency will involve inviting authorities from both the government and the public to establish a participation system. (6) The specific organizational structure, etc., will be immediately instructed to the three Cabinet secretaries for investigation and drafting, and submitted to the Four Ministers Conference for formal decision. (7) After the organization is decided, its official system will be submitted to the Privy Council for consultation. (8) The expenses will be included in the supplementary budget for the current year and must be realized within the current year.

Furthermore, from the perspective of national policy, this agency will be responsible for investigating and drafting the outline of the budget, but it will not establish a Budget Bureau and will not include a Personnel Bureau. (16th Kyodo News)

Bandit Disturbances in Eastern Suiyuan: Movements of Japanese Troops in North China; Advocate Suspending Sino-Japanese Diplomatic Negotiations; Treat the Suiyuan Incident as a Separate Issue 94

Tianjin Correspondence: Hashimoto, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army in Tianjin, Staff Officer Wachi, Attaché Tsukada, Aide-de-Camp Kawada, etc., returned to Tianjin on the 12th after visiting Han Fuju in Jinan. At 9:00 a.m. on the 13th, the Japanese Army Command held a special meeting, presided over by Commander Tasiro. All command staff, including Iida, Adachi, Tsuii, and Kai, as well as attaché Suzuki, Nagamine, and Sinagawa, attended. Mori Singichi, an attaché sent by the Kwantung Army Command, also attended the meeting and offered suggestions. Hashimoto and Wachi first reported on their inspection of Shandong and their meetings with Han Fuju and Shen Honglie. Then they began to discuss the situation in North China, economic development, and the issue of eastern Suiyuan. Finally, they decided on a reply to Tokyo's inquiry about Sino-Japanese diplomatic opinions. The meeting adjourned at 12:00. Mori Singichi left for Guanwai (Manchuria) on the night train of the 14th to report. In addition to specific policies on the economic development of eastern Suiyuan and Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the Japanese Army Command in Tianjin learned that during Staff Officer Ikeda's return to Japan to negotiate with various financial groups, the financial groups expressed their unwillingness to be controlled by the China Development Company, as it would limit their operations. They would only invest in the direction indicated by the Japanese Army Command if the China Development Company canceled the proposal to enhance its organization. Therefore, Tasiro deeply felt that this matter was clearly in opposition to the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) and that to make the China Development Company automatically abandon its plan to increase capital, it would be necessary to cooperate with the Kwantung Army Command. Therefore, he sent Chief of Staff Nagata to Changchun to meet with Itagaki to discuss the matter. Nagata telegraphed his reply to Tianjin on the 14th and will return on the 17th. At that time, the Japanese Army Command in Tianjin will hold another meeting to discuss and make a final decision. However, Mantetsu sent Director Sakatani Tsunekawa to Tianjin on the 13th to reside there, replacing the deceased Director Ishimoto, to assist the China Development Company in developing mineral resources. This again caused a head-on conflict with the Tianjin Japanese Army Command's intention to restrict the expansion of the China Development Company. It is still unknown how the Japanese Army Command will deal with it.

Regarding Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the Japanese central leadership, seeing that Kawagoe's meetings with our Foreign Minister Zhang have repeatedly failed to yield any hope of progress, fears that prolonged negotiations will damage the country's prestige. Therefore, they telegraphed the heads of the army, navy, and foreign affairs agencies in North China to solicit their opinions and subtly hinted at the possibility of immediately terminating the negotiations. On the morning of the 12th, Hashimoto and Wachi returned from Jinan and reported to Tasiro, who then exchanged opinions with the Japanese Consul General in Tianjin, Horiuchi, and the Chief of the Naval Intelligence Agency, Kubota. They agreed to terminate the negotiations, retain all pending cases, and wait for an opportunity to negotiate again. Therefore, according to the news circulating here, it can be determined that Kawagoe's meeting with Foreign Minister Zhang will, at most, go through one more time before they conclude this round of diplomacy. Tianjin also rumors that Kawagoe will return to Japan before the 25th of this month to report on the negotiation process. After this, Japan will continue to pursue its long-standing policy in North China, treating the Hebei-Chahar Political Council as its counterpart and entrusting the Japanese Army Command in Tianjin to handle matters directly at any time. This is because they want to achieve results quickly and no longer want to take a circuitous diplomatic route.

The Japanese Army Command in Tianjin still adheres to its principle of viewing the Suiyuan incident as a separate matter and makes no expression. All military actions on that side are entirely planned by the Kwantung Army Command. Although there have recently been battles in eastern Suiyuan, the territory of Hebei-Chahar remains as peaceful as ever. This is what the Japanese Army Command in Tianjin means by "treating it as a separate matter." (14th)

Military Center of Bandit-Puppet Forces in Northern Chahar: Now Moved to Bailingmiao and Shangdu; General Offensive on All Fronts Around the 20th of This Month; Wang Ying's Bandit Troops Will Invade Wuchuan and Guyang 95

Shangdu Correspondence: Li Shouxin, commander of the puppet army, is supervising the bandit-puppet forces to attack Suiyuan. The battle situation is quite fierce. By the afternoon of the 12th, it had eased slightly. It is heard that the puppet bandits' plan to attack Suiyuan has been decided: after a large army of a certain party and the newly trained elite from Jehol arrive at Bailingmiao, they will launch a general offensive on all fronts of Suiyuan around the 20th of this month, with a focus on the western Suiyuan route. Because Wang Ying's bandit troops are extremely familiar with the geography of western Suiyuan, Wang Ying's bandit troops will invade Wuchuan and Guyang, directly entering the Hetao region, while other routes will take a mobile disruption strategy to check the Suiyuan army's forces. Recently, Bailingmiao and Shangdu have become the military center of the bandit-puppet forces. The bandit-puppet troops gathered in Bailingmiao have reached more than 20,000. The firearms of Wang Ying's bandit troops in Shangdu have all been replaced with new guns and sent to Bailingmiao. The infantry of Zhang Wanqing's brigade can also be fully replaced after the 15th. Truth About Wang Jun's Fatal Plane Crash: Cause of Accident Was Due to Damaged Aircraft Parts; 3rd Army Temporarily Headed by Zeng Wanzhong as Acting Army Commander 96

Lanzhou Correspondence: Wang Jun, commander of the 3rd Army of the Army, took a military plane from Tianshui on the 9th of this month to Lanzhou to request instructions, intending to go to the front to supervise the suppression. Unexpectedly, when the plane flew to Langshitang, more than ten miles southeast of Maying in Tongwei, the aircraft parts suddenly broke, and it crashed and caught fire. Army Commander Wang and pilot Li Tuxian both suffered unexpected misfortunes. When the news spread, everyone was extremely shocked and mourned. Lanzhou received this bad news on the evening of the same day. Because the troops of the 3rd Army were suppressing bandits at the front, fearing that it would affect the morale of the army, it was not published until today. The details are supplemented as follows:

Coming to Lanzhou to Request Instructions

Because the troops of the 7th Division under Wang's command had arrived north of Jingyuan and Hui Ning from southern Longnan in the pursuit of the remaining bandits, and were about to continue pursuing the bandits on the Gansu-Ningxia border, Zhu Shaoliang, director of the Pacification Headquarters, telegraphed Wang to come to Lanzhou to discuss the strategy of suppressing the bandits. Upon receiving the telegram, Wang sent Chief of Staff Zhou Tiren to fly to Lanzhou on the No. 405 Douglas military plane on the 8th. The plane then flew back to Tianshui on the same day. Wang then took off from Tianshui at 9:05 a.m. on the 9th to come to Lanzhou. Only pilot Li Tuxian was on the same plane. Unexpectedly, at about 9:45 a.m., when they flew to Langshitang, more than ten miles southeast of Maying in Tongwei, the aircraft parts suddenly broke down, and the plane crashed and caught fire. Wang and the pilot were too seriously injured and died before they could be rescued.

After the Plane Crash

After this unexpected misfortune occurred, the Pacification Headquarters received telegrams from Wang, commander of the division in Tongwei, reporting the plane crash on the evening of the same day and the morning of the 10th. They immediately sent Deputy Adjutant Li Yuhua and Zhou Tiren, chief of staff of the 3rd Army, to the scene of the accident by car to collect the remains of Wang and the pilot.

Inspection of the Plane Crash

After Li and Zhou arrived at Langshitang, they immediately inspected the crashed plane. The fuselage had been completely burned, and the frame was also broken. The remains of Wang and the pilot were all trapped in the wreckage. Their bodies were charred by the fire, their limbs were broken, and their faces were blurred and difficult to identify. The situation was extremely tragic. Wang's personal military map, an antique box, and a shotgun that he carried with him, although partially burned, were still in the plane as his last relics. However, the pilot's eagle badge was still intact.

Moving the Coffin Back to Qin

Wang's remains were hastily placed in a coffin on the evening of the 10th. On the 11th, they were transported to Maying, where the local garrison officials and people from all walks of life held a temporary public memorial service in front of the coffin. On the 12th, the coffin was transported back to Qin by car. On the 13th, it was re-coffined, and his military personnel and relatives and family members handled the funeral affairs. After a public memorial service is held on a scheduled date, it will be transported back to its original home in Yunnan for burial.

Cause of the Accident

The pilot Li Tuxian, who was piloting the No. 405 military plane to Lanzhou this time, was from Liling, Hunan, and was 26 years old. He was a member of the Air Force's 4th Team and graduated from the Hunan Aviation Office and the Nanchang Air Force Training Corps. His piloting skills were originally very pure and he had never had an accident. He was always praised by his superiors. It is speculated that the cause of this accident was not poor piloting skills, and the weather between Lanzhou and Qin was sunny and windless on that day, so it can be judged that the aircraft parts suddenly broke down during the flight, the operation stopped or there was an oil leak and fire, leading to an unexpected misfortune that was unavoidable.

Shock and Mourning from All Sides

Lanzhou, Tianshui, Xi'an, Shanghai, and other places were shocked and mourned upon receiving this bad news. Wang's subordinates were deeply saddened. In addition to reporting to Chairman Chiang and the Xi'an Headquarters by telegram, Pacification Headquarters Director Zhu Shaoliang personally went to Tianshui on the morning of the 11th by a Boeing plane sent by Deputy Commander Zhang to comfort Wang's subordinates and his family. He is still in Qin and has not returned.

Army Commander's Position

The troops under Wang's command are the 7th and 12th Divisions. The commander of the 7th Division is Zeng Wanzhong, and the commander of the 12th Division is Tang Huaiyuan. They have been stationed in the Longnan area for the past two years and have been quite harmonious with the military and civilians. Recently, they have achieved remarkable results in suppressing bandits. After receiving the report of Wang's plane crash, Chairman Chiang ordered Zeng Wanzhong, the commander of the 7th Division of the army, to temporarily act as army commander, as the army was ordered to suppress bandits and the army commander's position could not be vacant for long.

Banking Sector Plans to Invest in Huai River Water Conservancy Project - Inter-Provincial Remittance Conference to be Held in Zhenjiang - 97

Wuhu Correspondence: Wancheng (Anhui Province) is located in the Yangtze and Huai River basins and has always been known for its abundant agricultural products. However, in recent years, it has suffered from droughts and floods, resulting in incalculable losses. The provincial authorities, in an effort to remedy this situation, have launched large-scale water conservancy projects throughout the province for the past two years (24th and 25th years of the Republic), aiming to prevent both droughts and floods. This spring, after the official establishment of the local bank, it has invested in and assisted in the completion of various riverfront water conservancy projects. It is also preparing to devote its economic resources to the construction and development of the Huai River area. Recently, after discussions between the bank and the provincial authorities, it was decided to implement the following projects: (1) Huai River Water Conservancy and Land Reclamation: In the Huai River region of northern Anhui, there are over 100,000 mu of fertile滩land suitable for mechanized agriculture, cultivating wheat and other grains. After repeated consultations between the Department of Finance and Construction and the local bank, it was decided that the local bank and other banks would invest over ten million yuan to engage in water conservancy projects and gradually reclaim the land. (2) Handling Simple Agricultural Product Mortgages: In recent years, various banks have been enthusiastically investing in rural areas, mainly through cooperatives and warehouse mortgages. However, many farmers still find it inconvenient. To regulate the rural economy and provide in-depth services to rural areas, the bank has decided to pilot simple mortgage loans. Under this method, farmers can mortgage rice and grains and store them in their own homes without having to transport them to a warehouse. However, they must obtain certification from the local保甲chief to receive the loan. The loan amount will be initially limited to five shi of rice and ten shi of paddy. The amount will be adjusted based on the implementation. (3) On Coordinating Local Finance Among Provinces: Local banks or provincial banks in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Jiangxi provinces have all expressed their agreement. Cheng Zhenji, the head of the Anhui local bank, has been instructed to write to Zhao Dihua, the director of the Jiangsu Department of Finance and the head of the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, to propose a conference in Zhenjiang to discuss inter-provincial remittance and the exchange of subsidiary coins. If effective methods are confirmed and implemented in the future, they will be extended to the provinces in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River and eventually throughout the country. (15th Day)

Fuzhou Unscrupulous Merchants Ship Rice to Taiwan - Rice Prices Rise Accordingly - Great Impact on People's Food Supply 99

Fuzhou Correspondence: The early rice crops in the coastal counties of this province suffered from several floods between spring and summer. Low-lying areas were inundated, and replanting was impossible, so the rice roots were removed to plant late rice. Fortunately, the weather and rainfall have been suitable. Last month, when the rice flowers bloomed, the weather was sunny and rainy, which was conducive to farming. After the crops matured, the weather was sunny, making it easier for the grains to solidify. According to people familiar with agriculture, the late rice crop is expected to be abundant. Farmers in various villages, as the autumn harvest is approaching, are selling off their stored grain, causing rice prices to fall by more than five jiao per shi. Rice is sold on the market for only nine yuan and three or four jiao per shi, while決rice is sold for only eight yuan and seven or eight jiao. Rice merchants believe that Fuzhou rice prices are two yuan lower than Shanghai rice prices and three yuan lower than Taiwan rice prices, so they are purchasing and transporting rice to Shanghai and Taiwan for sale. Except for rice transported to Shanghai, which is formally declared for export, the rice transported along the coast is loaded onto sailing ships and transported to Taiwan, which is more profitable than shipping to Shanghai. As a result, Fuzhou rice prices have recently risen by more than three or four jiao, which has affected the people's food supply. The Minhou County Party Department yesterday submitted a report to the Provincial Party Department requesting the Provincial Government to strictly prohibit rice exports to protect the national foundation and benefit the people. The report stated that the city's grain supply has always relied on the rice-producing areas of Fuding, Ningde, Lianjiang, and Luoyuan in eastern Fujian to provide assistance to the province, to avoid a shortage of grain between harvests. The city's rice and grain can only be imported, not exported. Now that the early rice crop is on the market, rice prices should fall to benefit the people. However, in recent days, there has been a continued upward trend. It is heard that unscrupulous rice merchants in Fuzhou, Ningde, Luoyuan, and other counties, as well as in the city, disregard the interests of the people and falsely claim to be transporting rice to Quanzhou and Shantou, but in reality, they are secretly transporting rice to Taiwan, where they can earn a profit of two or three yuan per shi of rice. In this time of national crisis, with the situation in East Asia tense, all Chinese people should actively store grain to help the country in case of emergency. However, they are not doing so, but instead damaging their own vitality and moving towards destruction, which will affect the country's survival and the people's livelihood. It is requested that your department promptly consult the provincial government to order an investigation and strictly prohibit unscrupulous merchants from exporting rice. If there are still cases of shipping rice to Taiwan, they should be severely punished to protect the national foundation and benefit the people. In addition, the price of flour in Fuzhou has also risen by about four jiao per bag due to the poor wheat harvest in the Americas and Canada. The current price for purchasing from Shanghai is three yuan, seven jiao, and eight fen per bag, plus two jiao for shipping and other expenses, so the selling price must be four yuan per bag. Fortunately, various flour mills in the city still have previously ordered goods, which have already yielded significant profits. Therefore, they are not following the current Shanghai market prices and are only selling at around three yuan and nine jiao in order to facilitate the circulation of goods and finance. However, due to the high price of flour, bread shops recently agreed to raise the price of bread by four wen per jin, while 包bread prices will not be raised, but the weight will be reduced.

Those with strong capital are buying as many dried cocoons as possible and stockpiling them in warehouses in preparation for opening in the spring. The current price of high white factory warp has risen to more than 850 yuan per package, and決silk has risen to 700 yuan. This is also good news for the future of silk cocoons.

Special District Rickshaw Guild Opposes Increasing License Fees, Deciding to Reduce Vehicles and Continue Negotiations 118

The Public Concession Public Works Bureau has decided to increase public rickshaw license fees from January 1st next year and reduce rickshaws by 500 on March 1st. The car dealers held a meeting yesterday to discuss it. The details are recorded below:

Increase License Fees and Reduce Car Rentals

Public rickshaw licenses are issued by the Public Works Bureau, the Public Concession Bureau, and the Public Works Bureau. The donation fee for the Public Concession is 2 yuan and 5 cents per month. Recently, the Public Works Bureau announced on October 22 that from January 1st next year, each license will be changed to 3 yuan and 5 jiao, which is an increase of 1 yuan and 4 jiao and 5 fen. However, for car rentals, it is stipulated that they will be reduced to a maximum of 7 jiao and 7 fen per day at the same time.

Reduce 500 Vehicles from Next Year

There were originally 10,000 public rickshaws in the Special District. Four years ago, 10 vehicles were cancelled by the Public Works Bureau due to a distant decree, so the actual number is only 9,990 vehicles. The bureau believes that rickshaws affect road traffic based on the recommendations of the Special Committee, so it decided to reduce 500 vehicles to 9,490 vehicles on March 1st next year. Although car dealers and rickshaw pullers have repeatedly requested opposition, there has been no result.

Yesterday's Meeting Discussed Negotiations and Opposition

Yesterday afternoon, the Special District Rickshaw Guild held a meeting. Gu Songmao, Hou Shao'an, Yin Zhiling, Bao Zhenhuang, Qiu Jixiang, Zheng Jian San, and others attended. Yin Zhiling presided over the meeting. After discussion, it was requested that the Special Committee on Rickshaws negotiate on the matter of increasing license fees, taking into account the difficulties of the merchants, and exempting it from implementation. As for the matter of reducing vehicles, according to the resolution of the general meeting, negotiations will continue.

China International Famine Relief Commission Celebrated its 15th Anniversary Yesterday, More Than 100 Chinese and Foreign Guests Attended, Changed its Future Working Guidelines and Raised 300,000 Yuan in Relief Funds 122

The China International Famine Relief Commission was established in Shanghai on November 16, 1921. Yesterday marked the 15th anniversary of its establishment. A commemorative meeting was held at the International General Association on Jing'an Temple Road at 7:30 PM yesterday. Chinese and foreign guests were invited to attend, to report on the principles and work of the association in the past. At the same time, a fundraising meeting was held. The details are recorded below:

Attending Guests

The guests who attended yesterday included Wu Tiecheng, Wang Zhengting (represented by Liu Yunfang), Yu Hongjun, Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Zhang Tingrong, Chen Guangfu, Li Dachao, Wei Wenbin, Liu Yuwan, Wang Yiting, Guo Chengen, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Liu Yunfang, and the Consuls of the United Kingdom, the United States, France, Germany, the Soviet Union, Denmark, Sweden, and Switzerland. There were more than 100 Chinese and foreign guests.

Work Report

Then a dinner party was held. After Liu Yunfang, representing Chairman Wang Zhengting, gave an opening speech, Guo Chengen reported on the association's past work, saying: (1) This association was established today in 1921, after a major drought in North China. At that time, although there were relief organizations in the country, they were not connected. Later, this association was formed. The general association was established in Beiping, and the original Chinese and foreign organizations were changed into branches. This is the process of its formation. (2) This association is a charitable organization jointly established by Chinese and foreign people. There is absolutely no political or religious boundary. Branches are established in 12 provinces including Shandong, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Guizhou, Yunnan, and Sichuan. Offices are established in Nanjing, Shanghai, and other places. This is the overview of the organization. (3) In terms of relief, this association not only saves the disasters that have already occurred, but also pays more attention to preventing future disasters. The goal of disaster prevention is construction. All things such as opening canals, digging wells, building roads and repairing embankments, and all kinds of facilities that facilitate people's livelihood are considered important tasks for disaster prevention. This is the so-called "construction relief" doctrine. (4) In the past 15 years, the association has spent more than 90 million yuan on emergency relief work. Larger projects include opening canals in the Weihe River in Shaanxi, digging wells in Hebei and Shandong provinces, and building embankments in Jiangxi, Hubei, Hebei, Henan, Shandong, and Anhui provinces. Other dredging of rivers has reached 290 miles, and building roads has reached 480 miles. The promotion of cooperatives, in particular, is pioneered by this association. As of April of this year, there were 2,865 cooperatives directly guided by this association, and the amount of loans to each cooperative reached 730,750 yuan.

Raising Huge Funds

At the same time, the holding of a fundraising meeting was announced. It is planned to raise 300,000 yuan, with Shanghai responsible for 100,000 yuan, and other places and overseas Chinese raising 200,000 yuan. The approval of the Ministry of Interior has already been obtained. As for the future improvement guidelines, three points have also been decided: (1) In the future, pay attention to rural construction projects. For rural highways and water conservancy, etc., assist those that are not covered by the national construction plan to promote their completion and facilitate rural areas. (2) Promote cooperative technology and help the Ministry of Industry promote cooperative undertakings. (3) Train disaster relief talents and float working staff to increase work efficiency. Finally, Mayor Wu gave a congratulatory speech, and Mr. An Xianjin gave a speech until 10 o'clock before everyone happily dispersed.

Mayor's Address

Today, the China International Famine Relief Commission is holding a 15th anniversary celebration. Tiecheng, as the honorary committee member of the Fundraising Committee of this association, is honored to attend the grand ceremony and gather with benevolent people from all walks of life at home and abroad. China has been plagued by disasters for many years, and the people have been displaced. Fortunately, benevolent people from all walks of life have been running around to provide relief out of their compassion, which has relieved the suffering of countless people and eliminated the hidden dangers of society. This merit is truly different from ordinary charitable acts. It is immeasurable to benefit the people and the country and the welfare of the people. Most of the work of this association is done by the efforts of friends from foreign countries. Tiecheng should propose and express his gratitude and admiration. "People drowning is like I drowning" and "People starving is like I starving." This is the embodiment of the inherent spirit of benevolence in China since ancient times. Since the establishment of this association, through the efforts of all of you for many years, this spirit has been carried forward. Tiecheng feels infinitely honored and gratified to follow you. However, the suffering of mankind is due to natural disasters on the one hand, and it is also caused by man-made disasters on the other hand. Before the organization of human society is reasonable, I am afraid that this suffering will be difficult to completely eliminate for a while. The world is still in a very turbulent and uneasy state. If we do not rush to save the future tragedies of mankind, we do not know where we will end up. This association is a group of benevolent people from various countries at home and abroad. I hope that we can carry forward the spirit of compassion and love that we have shown in the past 15 years, and launch a greater movement to eliminate the world's disasters invisibly. Then its benefits to the people will be endless. I wish you all good health and I wish you all greater success in your efforts.

Workers of Six Internal and External Cotton Factories Resumed Work 123

Factories in Shanghai and other places have not yet resumed work, Yufeng Yarn Factory is brewing

The striking workers of the three Japanese-owned factories in the Hudong District, including Dakang, Gongda, and Donghua, have all returned to work in the factory the day before yesterday. However, the workers in the fine yarn room of the Shanghai No. 2, 3, 4, and 5 factories, and the Tongxing No. 2 factory have not yet resumed work, and a labor unrest is also brewing in the Yufeng factory. The workers of the six internal and external cotton factories in the Huxi District resumed work in the factory yesterday morning because the factory has increased wages. The workers of the Huamei Printing and Dyeing Factory also resumed work at the same time. The details are recorded separately below:

Resumption of Work in Hudong Factories

The striking workers of the three Japanese-owned factories in the Hudong District, including Dakang, Gongda, and Donghua, have returned to work in the factory the day before yesterday after being earnestly persuaded by the party and government organs. There are still more than 300 workers in the fine yarn room of the Shanghai No. 2 and 3 factories and more than 300 workers in the reeling room who have not yet resumed work. More than 600 workers in the fine yarn room of the No. 4 and 5 factories have also not yet resumed work. Only half of the more than 2,500 workers in the day and night shifts of the Tongxing No. 2 factory have now resumed work. All the workers of the Yufeng Yarn Factory at the end of Yangshupu Road have also demanded an increase in wages. If the factory does not give a satisfactory reply, a labor unrest will inevitably occur. Therefore, the future of the labor unrest in the Japanese-owned yarn factories in the Hudong District is still difficult to quell.

Internal and External Six Factories Agree to Increase Wages

After the announcement of the strike by all the workers of the Internal and External Cotton No. 6 Factory in the West Suzhou River in the Huxi District, the party and government organs have sent people to persuade them, and the foremen have negotiated with the factory. Therefore, the factory has agreed to increase wages, and all the workers have entered the factory at 6:00 AM yesterday. The factory's notice is recorded as follows: "Our factory has already announced on November 14 that the wage increase is limited to 5%, which will be calculated from November 11. This is a special notice." It is also learned that the factory announced at the same time yesterday that the workers (No. 549), (No. 562), (No. 526), (No. 569), (No. 575), (No. 578), and (No. 634) have been dismissed. Upon hearing the news, the workers expressed their dissatisfaction with the factory's dismissal of workers without cause.

Workers of Meihua Dyeing Factory Resumed Work

After the strike by all the male and female workers of the Japanese-owned Meihua Printing and Dyeing Factory at No. 595 Hejian Road in the Hudong District, demanding an increase in wages, the labor and management sides negotiated on their own. As a result, it was decided to increase wages by 2% across the board. The remaining conditions will be negotiated again. All the workers have expressed their agreement with this condition, so it was decided to resume work in the factory at 6:00 AM yesterday.

Fine Yarn Workers of New Ewo Gunny Bag Factory Strike Against Wage Cuts, Workers' Representatives Arrested, Labor Side Proposes Conditions 124

The British-owned New Ewo Gunny Bag Factory next to the Yangshupu Water Plant employs more than 1,000 workers. There are now more than 300 connecting workers in the fine yarn room who are unable to make a living due to the exploitation of wage by the contractor. They demanded restoration, but failed to get what they wanted. Therefore, they jointly went on strike from 6:00 PM the day before yesterday (November 14) and put forward seven demands. The details are recorded below:

Strike Occurs

More than 300 connecting workers in the fine yarn room of the New Ewo Gunny Bag Factory used to earn 3 jiao and 5 fen per day. Recently, the contractors Ding Rongkun and Chen Asan unreasonably cut it to 2 jiao and 8 fen. Because they could not make a living, they demanded restoration, but failed to get what they wanted. Therefore, they went on strike from 6:00 PM the day before yesterday (November 14) to urge the contractors to realize their mistakes. However, because the workers have no organization, no one dares to come forward to negotiate. Then there were Qu A'er and Huang A'san who verbally guaranteed to the workers that the contractors would never oppress the workers and that representatives could be sent to the head office for negotiations. Cao Wanqing and Ji Shouhua were elected by the workshop to negotiate with Ding Rongkun, the general contractor. However, Ding refused in every possible way, resulting in no result. Therefore, at 7:00 AM yesterday, they went to Tao Bingnan's home, the head of the head office, for negotiations. Unexpectedly, Qu A'er and Huang A'san dragged the workers' representatives to the factory and beat them severely, and reported them to the Yulin Road Police Station, which detained the workers, who have not been released yet. Upon hearing the news, all the workers were indignant and held an emergency meeting yesterday, putting forward seven demands. If there is no result, they will continue to strike to urge the contractors to realize their mistakes.

Seven Demands

After the contractor reported the workers' representatives to the police station and detained them, all the workers expressed their indignation. Seven demands were put forward: (1) Immediately release the workers' representatives Cao Wanqing and Ji Shouhua. (2) Increase wages by 20%. (3) After working for two weeks, wages must be increased for two days, and shift work must be arranged every Sunday. (4) Give an additional 1 jiao for wiping each car. (5) Increase wages by 2 jiao per day per person for 8 taels of yarn. (6) No arbitrary fines or beatings of workers. (7) Request for the issuance of year-end bonuses at the end of the year. The above conditions have now been written by the labor side and directly submitted to the general foreman Smith, requesting him to accept them.

Promotion of Income Tax 127

Continued Consultation with Foreign Nationals

The Ministry of Finance is implementing income tax, and both Chinese and foreign nationals have a tax obligation. Previously, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs officially notified the embassies and consulates of various countries stationed in China to instruct foreign nationals to comply. The Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office has dispatched personnel to Shanghai to engage in multiple consultations with foreign nationals. Detailed explanations regarding collection methods and procedures have been provided, and general agreement has been obtained in principle. It is now understood that the British and American consulates and chambers of commerce in this city, recognizing that this tax is a sound global practice and that foreign residents in China should bear the obligation to pay, previously telegraphed their respective governments for instructions. Approval has now been received, indicating agreement. Therefore, there are no issues with British and American merchants paying taxes. As for other countries, no specific opinions have been expressed yet. The Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance's Income Tax Affairs Office has been collecting the second category of income tax since the first day of last month for over a month. The tax amounts payable by foreign nationals for October will be settled and collected. In addition to using diplomatic channels to continue consultations with various countries, the office will also send personnel to the chambers of commerce of various countries to urge collection. Furthermore, over sixty trainees from the direct tax personnel training class have now graduated and will be assigned to various locations by the Ministry of Finance starting next month.

Small Group Meeting of the Banking Sector

After the Ministry of Finance approved the postponement of the implementation of deposit interest income tax to New Year's Day next year, the Banking Association compiled the opinions from member banks of local banking associations and research from banking societies. A small group committee was formed for research. The committee member banks, including Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, Guohua Bank, Guohuo Bank, Continental Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Y盐业 Bank, Jincheng Bank, Zhejiang Xingye Bank, Zhejiang Shiye Bank, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Kenye Bank, Siming Bank, and Zhonghui Bank, fifteen in total, have all nominated committee members and reported to the Banking Association. It has been decided that after all reports are submitted, Pan Jiufen from the Bank of China will convene the first committee meeting.

Attendees of the Lecture Series

For the purpose of studying income tax, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, in conjunction with the Xu Yongzuo Accounting Firm, is jointly organizing an income tax lecture series, soliciting participation from industry and commerce. This lecture series is a public lecture, and anyone who joins only needs to pay a lecture fee of two yuan, without any other restrictions. The lecture period is three weeks, with three lectures per week, all held in the evening. The lecture notes have recently been printed. The lecture content is divided into ten lectures: The first lecture is on the meaning of income tax, explaining the principles of income tax; the second lecture is on the evolution of income tax, explaining the evolution of income tax systems in the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, Japan, Italy, Russia, and China; the third and fourth lectures are on China's current income tax system, explaining the types of taxation, tax amount calculation, tax procedures, payment methods, and penalties in China's current system; the fifth lecture is on income tax and capital, explaining the meaning of capital, public reserve funds, etc., in income tax law and the method of their calculation; the sixth lecture is on income tax and net profit, explaining the method of calculating net profit and its relationship to tax payment; the seventh lecture is on the valuation of assets for income tax purposes, explaining the rules for valuing various assets and their relationship to tax payment; the eighth lecture is on the accuracy of income tax amount and accounting, explaining the points that should be noted for the accuracy of tax amount in accounting; the ninth lecture is on income tax and accounting management; and the tenth lecture is on the improvement of bookkeeping system for income tax, guiding the points that should be improved in accounting management and bookkeeping system. It is said that these ten lectures will be given in rotation by Xu Yongzuo, the accountant, and his colleagues from the firm. Recently, many people from all walks of life have been enthusiastically signing up at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Xu Accounting Firm to join the lecture series.

Red Cross Society Raises Cotton Clothes for Northern Shaanxi 130

The Joint Office of the Chinese Southeast Associations of the World Red Cross Society received a telegram from Commanders Gao Guizi and He Shaonan of Northern Shaanxi, stating that Northern Shaanxi has suffered from banditry for years, homes are destroyed, and families are ruined. The disaster victims have no complete clothes and are starving. Many are dying of hunger and cold, requesting aid in the form of cotton clothes to save lives. The office believes that the disaster situation in Northern Shaanxi, which has suffered from both banditry and natural disasters, with widespread deaths, is no less severe than in Jiangxi. Relief should be provided as much as possible. Letters have been sent to various Southeast associations to raise funds together. However, the disaster area in Northern Shaanxi is vast, and there are many disaster victims. A small number of cotton clothes will not help. It is hoped that philanthropists at home and abroad will raise cotton clothes on their behalf, regardless of quantity, new or old, and send them to the association's office at No. 4 Tongfu Lane, Julai Road, French Concession, to be collected and transported to the disaster area for relief.

Grand Opening Ceremony of the Hujia and Sujia Highways: Over 400 Attendees, Including Chu Minyi and Wang Xiaolai 131

The Hujia and Sujia Highways, contracted to the China Merchants Bureau, were taken over on July 1st. A supplementary opening ceremony was held at 8:00 AM on November 15th at the Wuxing Main Station, and representatives from all walks of life in Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Jiaxing were invited to attend. Attendees included Chu Minyi, Wang Xiaolai, Shen Tianxin, Chen Qicai, Zhang Yipeng, County Magistrate Xu of Wujiang County, Xu Yuzheng representing the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, Zhu Zhengyuan representing the Two-Roads Administration Bureau, Jin Baishun, Huang Xiaofang, and Xu Shuqin, financial leaders of Hangzhou, Chen Cong, Director of the Zhejiang Transportation Administration, and over 400 representatives from all walks of life and the press. Chen Qinshi, the director of the Two-Roads Automobile Company, presided over the meeting and delivered the opening remarks. Xu Yuzheng representing the Zhejiang Construction Department, Chen Cong, Director of the Zhejiang Transportation Administration, Huang Renwang, Administrative Commissioner of the Wuxing District, Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee among the guests, Wang Zhengyuan, representing the Jing-Hang-Yong Two-Roads, and representatives of the Wuxing and Wujiang County Party Headquarters, delivered speeches one after another. It was mentioned that the opening of the Hujia and Sujia Highways will further develop the economy and culture of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces in the future, especially facilitating travel. The future development of the two roads was wished to be unlimited. After the chairman gave a speech in thanks, Mrs. Chen Cong performed the ribbon-cutting ceremony for the opening, and a photo session was held. The guests then boarded seven large buses and departed from the Hujia Road. A luncheon was held at the Zhenze Station Park. At this time, Chinese and foreign guests who came from Shanghai, Suzhou, and Jiaxing totaled no less than seven or eight hundred people. Chairman Chen and the directors entertained them separately. After the banquet, the guests to Lake, Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Shaoxing returned to Jiaxing. According to Director Chen, the Sujia Road is 73 kilometers long, and the Hujia Road is 58 kilometers long. The company leased them from the Construction Department. The Sujia Road lease fee is 5,000 yuan, and the Hujia Road deposit is 100,000 yuan, with a rent of 250,000 yuan and a lease term of 20 years. The Sujia Road was taken over in July of this year, and the Hujia Road cost a total of 530,000 yuan to build. It is expected that the company will lease it starting this month. Furthermore, the road was opened in February last year and completed in March this year. The capital of the two roads is 430,000 yuan. The company's shareholders are all well-known gentry merchants and financial leaders in Lake and Hangzhou. Therefore, the future development of the two roads will benefit the people immeasurably.

Yutang Celebrated Local Memorial Day Yesterday 132

Paying Homage to the Mi San Public Cemetery and Commemorative Parade

On November 16, 1929, Mr. and Mrs. Niu Yangsheng of Yutang, Shanghai, used the funds given by relatives and friends for the 100th birthday of their ancestor, Mi San, and Madam Wang, to establish the private Yutang Public Education Center, promoting public education. There were also the Qiangshu Horticulture School, Agricultural Training Class, and Women's Self-Help Society, all established and actively managed by private funding. Yutang, originally a remote area, has seen its business achieve results after many years of operation. In recent years, it has also been able to occupy a place in rural education, with some reputation. In recent years, the establishment of the Yongfu Industrial School, with its integration of industry and education, has also made practical contributions to rural education. Local people decided last year to designate November 16th each year as Yutang Local Memorial Day, which is the founding day of Yutang's educational cause. In addition to commemorating Mi San's birthday and the educational cause, meetings are also held on this day for research and to explore the progress of the cause. This year is the first time it is being held. Preparations have been made by the preparatory staff of the memorial meeting launched by various agencies in Yutang. It is reported that at 7:00 AM on the morning, staff of various agencies and residents of the teaching area held a tomb sweeping ceremony in front of the Wei San Public Cemetery. At 9:00 AM, they paraded in a line, and upon arrival, a brief report on the cause was given. The parade participants also raised questions about their respective causes within the prescribed time for mutual research. In the afternoon, a commemorative ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Education Center, with additional performances. A colored film was shown in the evening.

The Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui Unified Tax Bureau Actively Pursues Reforms 133

Since Sheng Shengyi was transferred to be the director of the Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui Unified Tax Bureau, he has spared no effort in reforming the tax policy. In order to fundamentally eradicate the accumulated malpractices of tax evasion, four inspectors have been added to the tax management offices in Ningbo, Haimen, Wenzhou, and other places for rotational inspection, implementing both overt and covert investigations. Furthermore, in order to save office time and increase the time for researching and reforming tax policies, following the methods of European and Western countries, all routine documents that are not urgent are sent by form. The reason only needs to be indicated on the form. The forms are divided into two types: A and B. "Delivery Certificate" is used for outports, and "Delivery Certificate" is used for the city. Each type is divided into original and duplicate sheets. If there is no special accident, the original sheet is filed, and the duplicate sheet is returned to the original presenting agency for record, without separate instructions. Since its implementation on October 1st, the office staff has found it convenient. In addition, a design committee has been organized within the bureau, with specialized personnel as members. The committee members are engaged in research on how to reform the tax policy and how to prevent smuggling, with the aim of being proper. The necessary expenses are all paid by the bureau director from his personal salary. Other investigations into privately made cigarettes (i.e., hand-cranked iron machines, wooden frames, etc.) and the selection and use of personnel are also being planned.

Shanghai Land Bureau Announces Measurement of Gaohang District Land 134

All Owners Should Pay Attention

Xu Fu, Director of the Shanghai Land Bureau, issued Announcement No. 20, stating: The bureau is now beginning to measure the land in Baos 22 and Tu 3 and Tūs 21, 22, 24, 28 and 29 of Gaohang District. All owners should pay attention to the following items: (1) The Dibao (local head) will distribute filling-out forms to the owners. The owners should fill them out truthfully within ten days after receiving the forms and have the Dibao collect them and submit them to Measurement Team 1 of the bureau at No. 26 Zhangjiaqiao Town East Road, Chenhang District, or the owners can directly submit them to the measurement team. (2) If the address of the owner is unknown, resulting in the filling-out form not being distributed, they can directly report to the bureau or Measurement Team 1 and fill it out themselves. (3) If the owner's field certificate is mortgaged elsewhere and cannot be filled out, the name and mu (unit of area) of the field certificate should be copied from the mortgagee immediately, without excuse. (4) When the land of each household is measured, the owner must, together with the Dibao, clearly point out the boundaries to the surveyor or measurer, or entrust a representative to point out the boundaries in advance. Otherwise, the bureau will only rely on the Dibao's guidance. If any errors or disputes arise in the future, the owner will be responsible. The above four items are related to the owner's consolidation of property rights. In addition to instructing the Dibao of each district to comply, it is hereby announced for general knowledge. All owners should pay special attention to this announcement.

Muslims Begin Month of Fasting Yesterday Morning 136

Muslims in this city are required to fast for one month every Ramadan (September) of the Islamic calendar (i.e., abstain from food). Yesterday marked the beginning of the month of Ramadan in the Islamic calendar, and Muslims gathered in mosques to bathe and pray before beginning the fast. Both men and women are required to fast. The time for fasting is from the moment the east is illuminated until the sun sets. During this time, eating, drinking, sexual intercourse, and all improper behavior are prohibited. Conditions that do not break the fast include forgetting to eat or drink, nocturnal emission, etc. Conditions that break the fast include intentionally eating, drinking, or having sexual intercourse during the day. However, sexual intercourse is not prohibited at night. The Quran states, "On the night of fasting, you may have intercourse with your wives. They are your garments, and you are their garments." Chapter 2, Verse 148. However, after sexual intercourse, a major ablution (i.e., bathing) is required. Every night at 7:00 PM during this month, Muslims in mosques across the city will hold prayers.

Jianghai Customs Uncovers Major Fraud Case: Lu Zhiqing Privately Makes Keys to Open Boxes and Steal Bills of Lading; Retrieves Goods from China Merchants Bureau and Sells Them for Profit; Seven Keys in Total; Previously Committed Multiple Offenses 137

Lu Zhiqing, a Ningbo native who previously worked as a customs broker at the Minli Customs Brokerage in this city, became unemployed. Familiar with customs declaration and shipping procedures, he knew that, according to custom, customs brokerages would first send the bills of lading to the customs authorities for inspection after the goods were imported and loaded onto the pier. To avoid brokers waiting for too long, the customs set up large iron storage boxes, numbered separately, to store the bills of lading of each brokerage. Each brokerage had its own key to open the box

according to the listed number

to retrieve the bills and ship the goods. When Lu was employed, he used lead to imitate the keys of various brokerages, totaling seven. Recently, due to extreme boredom, he came up with a whimsical idea to use the fake keys to open the boxes and fraudulently obtain goods. Most recently, he learned that the Jingji Customs Brokerage on Zilai Street in the French Concession was entrusted by Renfeng Hakka in Hankou to handle customs procedures in Shanghai. The Hakka entrusted the transportation of ten boxes of lotus seeds, worth 550 yuan,

to the China Merchants Bureau's Jiang'an Steamer.

When the ship arrived in port at 9:30 AM on the 9th of this month, the brokerage sent the bill of lading for the goods to the customs for inspection. When the customs issued the bill, Lu used the fake key to open the brokerage's storage box No. 741, took out the original bill, and at 3:00 PM on the 10th, hired two "Tiger Cars" from the Guangdng Road branch of the Anli Automobile Transportation Company at No. 64 Guangdong Road and transported the ten boxes of lotus seeds from the No. 17 warehouse of the China Merchants Bureau's South Pier. The two carters, Shi Jiayao and Ma San,

each carried five boxes

According to the address Lu provided, the cars went to No. 115 Hele Lane at the intersection of North Henan Road and Haining Road, where Qin Chang Printing Paper's Li Hui Rong was to receive the goods. When the first car arrived at the entrance of the lane, someone took the goods and transported them elsewhere. However, the car driven by Ma San was spotted by Chinese police officer No. 277 in the Hongkou area, who ordered the goods to be divided into two cars because they were overloaded. This caused a delay. When the divided car arrived at the destination again,

no one was there to receive the goods.

After searching everywhere for Li Hui Rong of Qin Chang, it was impossible to find him. They had no choice but to temporarily store the car at the Hongkou police station. This is the story of Lu's fraud. However, the Jingji Customs Brokerage had been waiting for the bill of lading without any news. It was not until the morning of the 11th that they inquired with the customs and learned that the bill of lading had been issued the day before. Fearing that it had been lost, they rushed to the China Merchants Bureau to stop the goods from being unloaded. Unexpectedly, the ten boxes of lotus seeds had been taken away with the bill the day before. They then learned that the bill was signed with

the words "Ke Zheng"

and stamped with the Anli Automobile Transportation Company seal. They reported the incident to the customs police station for investigation. The police station, recognizing the seriousness of the case, immediately dispatched detectives Cheng Yongnian, Wang Haiquan, Qu Hequi, Gu Wenkui, Liang Shenqing, Zhou Zenghua, and Hu Deqing to investigate separately. They first went to the Anli main branch on Dengtuo Road in the public concession to investigate. They learned that there was indeed a person named Wang Kezheng, who was the accountant at the Guangdong Road branch. They then worked with the central police station to bring Wang

and the carters, Shi and Ma,

who transported the stolen goods, to the police station. They testified that Lu Zhiqing instructed them to transport the goods. Lu used to hire an old carter named Gu when he worked at Minli, so he knew him. They were completely unaware that the lotus seeds were fraudulently obtained. The detectives then went to Minli to meet with manager Zhang Yongxing. They learned that Lu was introduced by Xie. Based on this clue, they set out to capture Lu. Lu fully admitted to the fraud, but

repeatedly lied

about the location of the stolen goods, causing the detectives to conduct empty searches multiple times. Finally, he revealed everything. According to his confession, five boxes of the original stolen goods were hidden in a vacant coffin on the upper floor of the Huiheji store at No. 129 Xueyuan Road, Guangqi Road in the city. They immediately worked with the Yimiao police station to recover the original stolen goods at the address. Some of them had already been sold. They also confiscated seven fake lead keys, three fake seals of customs brokerages, a cargo manifest from the Red Heart Canned Foods Company, and various customs brokerages'

cargo permits.

They also took Hui Yongfeng, the owner of the store, who was hiding the stolen goods, into custody. The detectives then asked Lu what he needed the Red Heart Canned Foods Company's cargo manifest for. Lu then confessed that on September 12th of this year, he had used the same method to fraudulently obtain ten boxes of grapes from Tongtai Customs Brokerage, each box containing forty-eight cans. Because he had nowhere to sell them, he falsely used the name of the Red Heart Company to sell them, and most of them had been sold. Only one hundred and seventy-nine cans

were recovered.

The seven keys that were obtained could open the storage boxes of the Jingji, Yongxingchang Dachang, Gongxing, Meisheng, Tongtai, Nantong, Tongfengtai, Taiguchang, and other brokerages. The detectives recovered all the remaining grapes and ordered the Jingji and Tongtai brokerages to claim the recovered stolen goods. Since Lu claimed that the fake keys could still open the iron boxes of other brokerages, fearing that other brokerages had also been defrauded, the two criminals were kept in custody for continued investigation to handle the case.

The Shanghai Municipal Zoo Pigeon Research Association held its tenth regular meeting at the meeting room of the Municipal Zoo yesterday afternoon. Shanghai-Hankou Navigation: Draft Restrictions Further Reduced 139

Load capacity around eleven feet, Wuhu water level only six feet

The Yangtze River water volume continues to decrease. The Wuhu water level on the Shanghai-Hankou section is only six feet. Details are as follows:

Decreasing Draft

The Customs Maritime Department received a report yesterday on the water levels along the Shanghai-Hankou section of the Yangtze River. The Hankou water level is only eight feet two inches, Jiujiang is only nine feet three inches, Anqing is only seven feet seven inches, and Wuhu is only six feet. Since these figures represent the number of feet above the lowest water level, according to the draft restrictions for ships announced by the Customs yesterday, only a load capacity of fourteen feet four inches is permitted for the Wuhu-Jiujiang section, and a load capacity of eleven feet eight inches is permitted for the Jiujiang-Hankou section. Therefore, navigation on the Shanghai-Hankou section is extremely difficult.

Marine Police Announcement

The Customs Patrol and Works Department issued the following marine police announcement for the lower Yangtze River yesterday: Received a telegram from the River Affairs Department (accuracy to be verified) as follows: "The shallowest water volume in the Jiangxinzhou channel was 7.92 meters (26 feet) on the 13th of this month, while the Wuhu water gauge marker was 1.74 meters (5.7 feet). The shallowest water volume in the Luohuzhou channel was 5.79 meters (19 feet) on the 14th of this month, while the Hankou water gauge marker was 1.62 meters (8.06 feet). The shallowest water volume in the east channel of Daijiazhou was 1.966 feet (13 feet) on the 15th of this month, while the Hankou water gauge marker was 2.56 meters (8.4 feet)." (Signed) Carnell, Customs Maritime Patrol and Works Department.
